This will apply a set of colours (which can be changed) to the tags in the order that they are defined.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eHighlighting tags is configurable. Use \u003ccode\u003edefaultHighlight\u003c/code\u003e to set up highlights for all tags. If you need to configure individual tags differently, use \u003ccode\u003ecustomHighlight\u003c/code\u003e. If settings are not specified in \u003ccode\u003ecustomHighlight\u003c/code\u003e, the value from \u003ccode\u003edefaultHighlight\u003c/code\u003e is used.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eCustom highlights can also be specified for sub tags (if used).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: \u003ccode\u003edefaultHighlight\u003c/code\u003e is not applied to sub tags.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBoth \u003ccode\u003edefaultHighlight\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ecustomHighlight\u003c/code\u003e allow for the following settings:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eforeground\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the foreground colour of the highlight in the editor and the marker in the ruler.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebackground\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the background colour of the highlight in the editor.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: Foreground and background colours can be specified using \u003ca href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_colors\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eHTML/CSS colour names\u003c/a\u003e (e.g. \"Salmon\"), RGB hex values (e.g. \"#80FF00\"), RGB CSS style values (e.g. \"rgb(255,128,0)\" or colours from the current theme, e.g. \u003ccode\u003epeekViewResult.background\u003c/code\u003e. See \u003ca href=\"https://code.visualstudio.com/api/references/theme-color\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eTheme Color\u003c/a\u003e for the details. Hex and RGB values can also have an alpha specified, e.g. \"#ff800080\" or \"rgba(255,128,0,0.5)\".\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eopacity\u003c/code\u003e - percentage value used with the background colour. 100% will produce an opaque background which will obscure selection and other decorations.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: opacity can only be specified when hex or RGB colours are used.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003efontWeight\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003efontStyle\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etextDecoration\u003c/code\u003e - can be used to style the highlight with standard CSS values.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eborderRadius\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the border radius of the background of the highlight.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eicon\u003c/code\u003e - used to set a different icon in the tree view. Must be a valid octicon (see \u003ca href=\"https://octicons.github.com\"\u003ehttps://octicons.github.com\u003c/a\u003e) or codicon (see \u003ca href=\"https://microsoft.github.io/vscode-codicons/dist/codicon.html\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ehttps://microsoft.github.io/vscode-codicons/dist/codicon.html\u003c/a\u003e). If using codicons, specify them in the format \"$(\u003cem\u003eicon\u003c/em\u003e)\". The icon defaults to a tick if it's not valid. You can also use \"todo-tree\", or \"todo-tree-filled\" if you want to use the icon from the activity view.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eiconColour\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the colour of the icon in the tree. If not specified, it will try to use the foreground colour or the background colour. Colour can be specified as per foreground and background colours, but see note below.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: Theme colours are only supported when using codicons. Hex, RGB and HTML colours are only supported when using octicons or the default icon.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003egutterIcon\u003c/code\u003e - set to true to show the icon in the editor gutter.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: Unfortunately, only octicons and the todo-tree icon can be displayed in the gutter.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erulerColour\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the colour of the marker in the overview ruler. If not specified, it will default to use the foreground colour. Colour can be specified as per foreground and background colours.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erulerOpacity\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the opacity of the ruler markers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: Only works with hex and RGB colour settings.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003erulerLane\u003c/code\u003e - used to set the lane for the marker in the overview ruler. If not specified, it will default to the right hand lane. Use one of \"left\", \"center\", \"right\", or \"full\". You can also use \"none\" to disable the ruler markers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e - used to control how much is highlighted in the editor. Valid values are:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etag\u003c/code\u003e - highlights just the tag\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etext\u003c/code\u003e - highlights the tag and any text after the tag\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etag-and-comment\u003c/code\u003e - highlights the comment characters (or the start of the match) and the tag\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etag-and-subTag\u003c/code\u003e - as above, but allows the sub tag to be highlight too (with colours defined in custom highlights)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etext-and-comment\u003c/code\u003e - highlights the comment characters (or the start of the match), the tag and the text after the tag\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eline\u003c/code\u003e - highlights the entire line containing the tag\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewhole-line\u003c/code\u003e - highlights the entire line containing the tag to the full width of the editor\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecapture-groups:n,m...\u003c/code\u003e - highlights capture groups from the regex, where 'n' is the index into the regex\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003enone\u003c/code\u003e - disable highlightling in the document\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehideFromTree\u003c/code\u003e - used to hide tags from the tree, but still highlight in files\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehideFromStatusBar\u003c/code\u003e - prevents the tag from being included in the status bar counts\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehideFromActivityBar\u003c/code\u003e - prevents the tag from being included in the activity bar badge count\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026quot;todo-tree.highlights.defaultHighlight\u0026quot;: {\n    \u0026quot;icon\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;alert\u0026quot;,\n    \u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: }\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.highlights.defaultHighlight\"\u003c/span\u003e: {\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"icon\"\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003ered\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"background\"\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.highlights.customHighlight\"\u003c/span\u003e: {\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"TODO\"\u003c/span\u003e: {\n        \u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003etrue\u003c/span\u003e\n    }\n}\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: The highlight configuration is separate from the settings for the search. Adding settings in \u003ccode\u003ecustomHighlight\u003c/code\u003e does not automatically add the tags into \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.general.tags\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e*Note: Using the \u003ccode\u003ecapture-groups\u003c/code\u003e setting in \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e may have an impact on performance with large files.\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe tree view header can contain the following (default)\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\" href=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Gruntfuggly/todo-tree/master/resources/button-icons/filter.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Gruntfuggly/todo-tree/master/resources/button-icons/filter.png\" alt=\"filter\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e - Only show items in the tree which match the entered filter text\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\" href=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Gruntfuggly/todo-tree/master/resources/button-icons/clear-filter.png\"\u003e\u003cimg view will bring up a context menu with the following options:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHide This Folder/Hide This File\u003c/strong\u003e - removes the folder or file from the tree\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eOnly Show This Folder\u003c/strong\u003e - remove all other folders and subfolders from the tree\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eOnly Show This Folder And Subfolders\u003c/strong\u003e - remove other folders from the tree, but keep subfolders\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eReset Folder Filter\u003c/strong\u003e - reset any folders previously filtered using the above\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eToggle Badges\u003c/strong\u003e - enable/disable SCM decorations\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eToggle Compact Folders\u003c/strong\u003e - enable/disable compressed folder names\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eToggle Item Counts\u003c/strong\u003e - enable/disable counts of tags\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eScan Open Files Only\u003c/strong\u003e - show TODOs from files open in VSCode (no search)\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eScan Current File Only\u003c/strong\u003e - show TODOs from the current open file only\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eScan Workspace And Open Files\u003c/strong\u003e - show TODOs from the workspace and any open files\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eScan Workspace Only\u003c/strong\u003e - show TODOs from the workspace only (requires manual refresh)\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eExpand Tree/Collapse Tree\u003c/strong\u003e - expand or collapse the whole tree\n\u003cstrong\u003eShow Tree View/Show Flat View/Show Tags Only View\u003c/strong\u003e - change the tree view style\n\u003cstrong\u003eGroup by Tag/Ungroup by Tag\u003c/strong\u003e - toggle grouping of items by tag\n\u003cstrong\u003eGroup by Sub Tag/Ungroup by Sub Tag\u003c/strong\u003e - toggle grouping of items by sub tag\n\u003cstrong\u003eExport Tree\u003c/strong\u003e - dump the tree contents into a file\n\u003cstrong\u003eReveal Current File in Tree\u003c/strong\u003e - show the current editor file in tree (if present)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: The current filters are shown in the debug log. Also, the filter can always be reset by right clicking the \u003cstrong\u003eNothing Found\u003c/strong\u003e item in the tree. If your tree becomes invisible because everything is filtered and \u003ccode\u003ehideTreeWhenEmpty\u003c/code\u003e is set to true, you can reset the filter by pressing \u003cstrong\u003eF1\u003c/strong\u003e and selecting the \u003cstrong\u003eTodo Tree: Reset Folder Filter\u003c/strong\u003e command.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe commands \u003cstrong\u003eTodo Tree: Go To Next\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003eTodo Tree: Go To Previous\u003c/strong\u003e can be used to move to the next and previous TODO within the current editor.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eConfiguration\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-configuration\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Configuration\" href=\"#configuration\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe extension can be customised as follows (default values in brackets):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.debug\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nShow a debug channel in the output view.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.periodicRefreshInteval\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nInterval (in minutes) for automatically refreshing the tree. Set to '0' to disable, or to the number of minutes between refreshes. \u003cem\u003eNote: This is not typically needed as the tree will be refreshed when files change.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.automaticGitRefreshInterval\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nPolling interval (in seconds) for automatically refreshing the tree when your repository is updated. This will check if your repository HEAD has changed and trigger a rescan of the workspace if it has. This replaces the file watcher functionality. Set to '0' to disable, or to the number of seconds between checks.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.exportPath\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e~/todo-tree-%Y%m%d-%H%M.txt\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nPath to use when exporting the tree. Environment variables will be expanded, e.g \u003ccode\u003e${HOME}\u003c/code\u003e and the path is passed through strftime (see \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/samsonjs/strftime\"\u003ehttps://github.com/samsonjs/strftime\u003c/a\u003e). Set the extension to \u003ccode\u003e.json\u003c/code\u003e to export as a JSON record.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.rootFolder\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e\"\"\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nBy default, any open workspaces will have a tree in the view. Use this to force another folder to be the root of the tree. You can include environment variables and also use ${workspaceFolder}. e.g.\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003ccode\u003e\"todo-tree.general.rootFolder\": \"${workspaceFolder}/test\"\u003c/code\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nor\u003cbr\u003e\n\u003ccode\u003e\"todo-tree.general.rootFolder\": \"${HOME}/project\"\u003c/code\u003e.\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: Other open files (outside of the rootFolder) will be shown (as they are opened) with their full path in brackets.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.schemes\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e['file','ssh','untitled']\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nEditor schemes to find TODOs in. To find TODOs in settings files, for instance, add \u003ccode\u003evscode-userdata\u003c/code\u003e or for output windows, add \u003ccode\u003eoutput\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.tags\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e[\"TODO\",\"FIXME\",\"BUG\"]\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nThis defines the tags which are recognised as TODOs. This list is automatically inserted into the regex.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.general.tagGroups\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e{}\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nThis setting allows multiple tags to be treated as a single group. Example:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"    \u0026quot;todo-tree.general.tagGroups\u0026quot;: {\n        \u0026quot;FIXME\u0026quot;: [\n            \u0026quot;FIXME\u0026quot;,\n            \u0026quot;FIXIT\u0026quot;,\n            \u0026quot;FIX\u0026quot;,\n        ]\n    },\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.general.tagGroups\"\u003c/span\u003e: {\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"FIXME\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eFIXME\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eFIXIT\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eFIX\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n        ]\n    },\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis treats any of \u003ccode\u003eFIXME\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eFIXIT\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eFIX\u003c/code\u003e as \u003ccode\u003eFIXME\u003c/code\u003e. When the tree is grouped by tag, all of these will appear under the \u003ccode\u003eFIXME\u003c/code\u003e node. However if you want to refine it, make sure that the \u003ctt\u003e($TAGS)\u003c/tt\u003e is kept as \u003ctt\u003e($TAGS)\u003c/tt\u003e will be replaced by the expanded tag list. Anything that the regex matches will be removed from the text. If a capture group is included, the contents are extracted into a sub tag, which will be used in the tree to group similar tags. The sub tag can also be used as a placeholder in \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.tree.subTagClickUrl\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.tree.labelFormat\u003c/code\u003e. Sub tags can also be highlighted by specifying a section in the \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.highlights.customHighlights\u003c/code\u003e setting. To highlight the sub tag itself, set \"type\" to \"tag-and-subTag\" in custom highlights for the tag.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExamples:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\"^:\\s*\"\u003c/code\u003e can be used to remove colons from immediately after tags.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\"^\\s*\\((.*)\\)\"\u003c/code\u003e can be used to extract anything in parentheses after the tag and use it as a sub tag.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.regex.regexCaseSensitive\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nSet to false to allow tags to be matched regardless of case.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.ripgrep.ripgrep\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e\"\"\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nNormally, the extension will locate ripgrep itself as and when required. dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.tree.labelFormat\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e${tag} ${after}\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nFormat of the TODO item labels. Available placeholders are \u003ccode\u003e${line}\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e${column}\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e${tag}\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e${before}\u003c/code\u003e (text from before the tag), \u003ccode\u003e${after}\u003c/code\u003e (text from after the tag), \u003ccode\u003e${filename}\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e${filepath}\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e${afterOrBefore}\u003c/code\u003e (use \"after\" text or \"before\" text if after is empty). When using \u003ccode\u003e${tag}\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e${subTag}\u003c/code\u003e you can also transform the text with \"uppercase\", \"lowercase\" or \"capitalize\", e.g. \u003ccode\u003e${tag:lowercase}\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etodo-tree.tree.scanMode\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003eworkspace\u003c/code\u003e)\u003cbr\u003e\nBy default the extension scans the whole workspace (\u003ccode\u003eworkspace\u003c/code\u003e). href=\"#multiline-todos\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf the regex contains \u003ccode\u003e\\n\u003c/code\u003e, then multiline TODOs will be enabled. In this mode, the search results are processed slightly differently. If results are found which do not contain any tags from \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.general.tags\u003c/code\u003e it will be assumed that they belong to the previous result that did have a tag. For example, if you set the regex to something like:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026quot;todo-tree.regex.regex\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;(//)\\\\s*($TAGS).*(\\\\n\\\\s*//\\\\s{2,}.*)*\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.regex.regex\"\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e(//)\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es*($TAGS).*(\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003en\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es*//\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es{2,}.*)*\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis will now match multiline TODOs where the extra lines have at least two spaces between the comment characters and the TODO item. e.g.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"// TODO multiline example\n//  second line\n//  third line\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e// TODO multiline example\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e//  second line\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e//  third line\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you want to match multiline TODOs in C++ style multiline comment blocks, you'll need something like:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026quot;todo-tree.regex.regex\u0026quot;: class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es{2,}.*)*\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ewhich should match:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"/* TODO multiline example\n**  second line\n**  third line\n*/\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e/* TODO multiline example\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e**  second dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: If you are modifying settings using the settings GUI, you don't need to escape each backslash.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWarning: Multiline TODOs will not work with markdown TODOs and may have other unexpected results. There may also be a reduction in performance.\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eExcluding files and folders\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-excluding-files-and-folders\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Excluding files and folders\" href=\"#excluding-files-and-folders\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo restrict the set of folders which is searched, you can define \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.filtering.includeGlobs\u003c/code\u003e. This is an array of globs which the search results are matched against. If the results match any of the globs, they will be shown. By default the array is empty, which matches everything. See \u003ca href=\"https://code.visualstudio.com/api/references/vscode-api#GlobPattern\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ehere\u003c/a\u003e for more information on globs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: globs paths are absolute - not relative to the current workspace.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo exclude folders/files from your search you can define \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.filtering.excludeGlobs\u003c/code\u003e. If the search results match any of these globs, then the results will be ignored.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can also include and exclude folders from the tree using the context menu. This folder filter is applied separately to the include/exclude globs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: By default, ripgrep ignores files and folders from your \u003ccode\u003e.gitignore\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e.ignore\u003c/code\u003e files. If you want to include these files, set\u003c/em\u003e \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.ripgrep.ripgrepArgs\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003eto\u003c/em\u003e \u003ccode\u003e--no-ignore\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/sup\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMarkdown Support\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-markdown-support\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Markdown Support\" href=\"#markdown-support\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen the extension was first written, very basic markdown support was added simply by adding a pattern to the default regex to match \"\u003ccode\u003e- [ ]\u003c/code\u003e\". A better way to handle markdown TODOs is to add \"\u003ccode\u003e(-|\\d+.)\u003c/code\u003e\" to the list of \"comments\" in the first part of the regex and then adding \"\u003ccode\u003e[ ]\u003c/code\u003e\" and \"\u003ccode\u003e[x]\u003c/code\u003e\" to the list of tags in \u003ccode\u003esettings.json\u003c/code\u003e, e.g. :\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026quot;todo-tree.regex.regex\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;(//|#|\u0026lt;!--|;|/\\\\*|^|^\\\\s*(-|\\\\d+.))\\\\s*($TAGS)\u0026quot;\n\u0026quot;todo-tree.general.tags\u0026quot;: [\n        \u0026quot;BUG\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;HACK\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;FIXME\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;TODO\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;XXX\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;[ ]\u0026quot;,\n        \u0026quot;[x]\u0026quot;\n    ]\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.regex.regex\"\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e(//|#|\u0026lt;!--|;|/\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003e*|^|^\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es*(-|\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003ed+.))\u003cspan class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003es*($TAGS)\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"todo-tree.general.tags\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eBUG\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eHACK\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n    ]\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csup\u003e\u003cem\u003eNote: If you modify the settings via the GUI, replace every instance of\u003c/em\u003e \u003ccode\u003e\\\\\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003ein the regex setting with\u003c/em\u003e defines the tags using the \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.general.tags\u003c/code\u003e setting. Older versions of the extension had the tags directly defined in the \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.regex.regex\u003c/code\u003e whereas now, the regex replaces \u003cstrong\u003e$TAGS\u003c/strong\u003e with the contents of \u003ccode\u003etodo-tree.general.tags\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eGrouping by tag doesn't work for markdown task list items as there is no tag to group with. aria-describedby=":R5v6fal9lab:-loading-announcement" id=":R5v6fal9lab:"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="octicon octicon-kebab-horizontal" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16" height="16"
